ECCANG WMS API Documentation

Complete English reference for the ECCANG WMS API. Covers developer guide, basic data, products, inbound orders, orders, returns, FBA, billing, and more.

131
API Endpoints
17
Modules
SOAP
Protocol
Developer Guide — 开发者必读
Integration Guide 接入指南 Developer Guide

Access Guide

1.1 WSDL Address

Production: http://domain/default/svc/wsdl

1.2 Service Address (curl data)

Production: http://domain/default/svc/web-service

1.3 Common Request Information

Common Request Parameters
ParameterTypeRequiredDescription
appTokenStringYesAPI key
appKeyStringYesAPI identifier
serviceStringYesAPI method, refer to method list
languageenumNozh_CN, en_US (information language)
paramsJsonStringNoRequest data content in JSON format
Error Format
ParameterTypeRequiredDescription
errMessageStringYesError message content
errCodeStringYesError code
Pagination Format
ParameterTypeRequiredDescription
pageSizeStringYesPage size
pageStringYesCurrent page
Changelog 更新日志 Developer Guide
VersionUpdate DateDescription
2.22021/09/14Create or edit inbound order: added entiry_code field
2.12021/01/26Create or edit FBA order: modified attach_type description in createOrEditFbaOrder
2.02017/01/19Get billing detail: getBillingDetail
1.62016/10/22Order-related interfaces such as createOrder, modifyOrder: added platform_shop platform store
1.52016/08/11createProduct, modifyProduct, getProductList interfaces: added attributes
1.42015/10/15Added product_declared_name_zh (Chinese declared product name) attribute
1.32015/05/05getOrderByRefCode interface
1.22014/12/25Optimization
1.12014/07/08createOrder, modifyOrder interfaces: added forceVerify attribute for mandatory verification
1.02014/05/12Initial API documentation created
Basic Data — 获取基础数据
Warehouse List 系统仓库 Basic Data

getWarehouse

Home > Get Basic Data > System Warehouse

---

Request

Parameter NameData TypeRequiredDescription
pageSizeIntOptionalNumber of records per page; if omitted, all records are queried
pageIntOptionalCurrent page number; if omitted, all records are queried

---

Response

Parameter NameData TypeDescription
askstringRefer to common response parameters
messagestringRefer to common response parameters
paginationObjectRefer to pagination format
countIntTotal number of records
nextPageStringIndicates if there is a next page; "true" means yes, "false" means no
dataObjectData content
ErrorObjectRefer to Error format

---

data Parameters

Parameter NameData TypeDescription
warehouse_idintWarehouse ID
warehouse_codestringWarehouse code
warehouse_namestringWarehouse name
country_codestringTwo-letter country code where the warehouse is located
warehouse_typeintWarehouse type: 0 = Standard, 1 = Transit, 2 = Virtual
warehouse_statusintWarehouse status: 0 = Unavailable; 1 = Available; 2 = Disabled
country_idintCity ID
postcodestringPostal code
statestringProvince
citystringCity
street_address1stringContact address line 1
street_address2stringContact address line 2
street_numberstringStreet number
is_distribute_warehouseIntWhether it is a distribution warehouse; 1 = Yes, 0 = No
areastringDistrict/County
emailstringEmail
company_namestringCompany name
contact_personstringContact person
TelephonestringTelephone

---

SOAP XML Examples

Request Example:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<SOAP-ENV:Envelope xmlns:SOAP-ENV="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/" xmlns:ns1="http://www.example.org/Ec/">
    <SOAP-ENV:Body>
        <ns1:callService>
            <paramsJson>
                {
                    "pageSize":"1",
                    "page":1
                }
            </paramsJson>
            <appToken>appToken</appToken>
            <appKey>appKey</appKey>
            <service>getWarehouse</service>
        </ns1:callService>
    </SOAP-ENV:Body>
</SOAP-ENV:Envelope>

Response Example:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<SOAP-ENV:Envelope xmlns:SOAP-ENV="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/" xmlns:ns1="http://www.example.org/Ec/">
    <SOAP-ENV:Body>
        <ns1:callServiceResponse>
            <response>
                {
                    "ask":"Success",
                    "message":"Success",
                    "refId":"",
                    "pagination":
                        {
                            "page":"1",
                            "pageSize":"1"
                        },
                    "count":"3",
                    "nextPage":"true",
                    "data":[
                        {
                            "warehouse_id":"1",
                            "warehouse_code":"HRBW",
                            "warehouse_type":"0",
                            "warehouse_status":"1",
                            "country_id":"49",
                            "state":"黑龙江",
                            "city":"哈尔滨",
                            "contacter":"",
                            "company":"",
                            "phone_no":"",
                            "street_address1":"",
                            "street_address2":"",
                            "zipcode":"",
                            "warehouse_desc":"哈尔滨仓",
                            "is_distribute_warehouse":"1",
                           "mail": "173881122@qq.com123",
                            "company_name": "易仓科技",
                            "contact_person": "张小明",
                            "telephone": "18556566965",
                            "area": "深圳区县"
                        }
                    ]
                }
            </response>
        </ns1:callServiceResponse>
    </SOAP-ENV:Body>
</SOAP-ENV:Envelope>

Request

Response

response Parameters

ParameterData TypeDescription
askstringRefer to common response parameters
messagestringRefer to common response parameters
dataObjectData content
ErrorObjectRefer to Error format

data Parameters

ParameterData TypeDescription
company_codestringCompany code
company_namestringCompany name
account_balancestringAvailable account balance
freeze_amountstringFrozen amount in the account
currencystringCurrency
firstnamestringFirst name
lastnamestringLast name
emailstringEmail address
telephonestringTelephone number
faxstringFax number

Request Example:

<SOAP-ENV:Envelope xmlns:SOAP-ENV="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/" xmlns:ns1="http://www.example.org/Ec/">
    <SOAP-ENV:Body>

Request

Response

paramsJson Parameters

Parameter NameData TypeRequiredDescription
file_typestringRequiredFile type, supported types are defined as follows:
Label (order_label): pdf, png, gif, jpg, jpeg
Attachment (order_attach): zip, rar, pdf, png, gif, jpg, doc, docx, xls, xlsx
Carton Mark (other_documents_carton): pdf, png, jpg, jpeg, gif
Invoice (other_documents_invoice): pdf, png, jpg, jpeg, gif
file_datastringRequiredFile data in base64 format
modulestringRequiredSupports order attachments, order labels, other attachments carton marks, other attachments invoices. Enumeration values:
order_attach (Order Attachment)
order_label (Order Label)
other_documents_carton (Other Attachments Carton Mark)
other_documents_invoice (Other Attachments Invoice)
If the label is in PDF format, please use order_label
need_to_printintOptionalWhether printing is required when module is order_attach (Order Attachment). 0 - No, 1 - Yes. Only applicable for image and PDF files.
file_notestringOptionalFile description (0-255 characters)
file_urlstringOptionalFile URL. When using file_url, file_data can be omitted

expiration_datedateOptionalExpiration date, format: YYYY-MM-DD
operate_typeint(1)RequiredOperation type:<br>0: PDF (Barcode);<br>1: PDF (QR code)
print_sizeint(2)RequiredPrint size:<br>1: 100*100;<br>2: 100*30;<br>3: 100*60;<br>4: 50*30;<br>5: 70*30;<br>6: A4 (3);<br>7: A4 (4);<br>8: 90*30;<br>9: A4 (3*9 new);<br>10: A4 (3*8);<br>11: US Letter (3);<br>12: US Letter (4)<br>Note: Default is 1 if not provided
print_code_typestring(50)RequiredPrint code type:<br>1: Product barcode<br>2: Product SKU<br>3: Custom code<br>4: Internal code<br>5: Product barcode + Internal code
extra_print_infostring(30)RequiredAdditional information to print (multiple values supported, separated by commas):<br>1: Product name<br>2: Customer code<br>3: Product barcode<br>4: Product SKU<br>5: Custom code<br>6: Made in China<br>7: Date<br>8: Separator<br>9: Product name (EN)

bulk_cargo_type_pieceInt(1)OptionalBulk cargo type (piece): 0 = no; 1 = yes; default 0 (custom interface parameter; if enabled, mutually exclusive with container_type and bulk_cargo_type)
stock_typeInt(1)OptionalInbound order stock type: default 0 = warehouse-based; 1 = standard area; 2 = temporary storage area; 5 = box-based (Note: the first three stock types apply at order level, all boxes have the same stock type; box-based stock type is used in combination with item.inventory_type parameter)
itemsarrayRequiredInbound order details

---

items Parameters

Parameter NameData TypeRequiredDescription
product_skustring(80)RequiredSKU
quantityint(11)RequiredQuantity
box_noint(64)RequiredBox number
product_pricedecimal(10,3)OptionalProduct unit price (converted to customer currency)
currency_codestring(32)OptionalProduct currency (this currency will be converted to customer currency)
associated_barcodestring(100)OptionalAssociated barcode; not mandatory; the same SKU in one inbound order can only have one associated barcode; different SKUs must have different associated barcodes
product_datedateOptionalProduct manufacture date
expiration_datedateOptionalProduct expiration date, format YYYY-MM-DD
product_batch_codeString(50)OptionalProduct batch attribute code
inventory_typeint(1)OptionalBox-level inventory type: 0 = warehouse confirmation; 1 = standard; 2 = temporary storage (when stock_type=5, treated as warehouse confirmation; note that the same box number must have consistent inventory type; if box-level inventory type is not passed, default is warehouse confirmation; for other stock_type values, box-level inventory type should be consistent with stock_type)

---

Get Inbound Order PDF 获取入库单PDF文件 Inbound Orders

getReceivingBoxPdfByCode

Home > Receiving Order Module > Get Receiving Order PDF File

---

Request

Response

---

paramsJson Parameters

Parameter NameData TypeRequiredDescription
receiving_codeStringRequiredReceiving order number
pdf_typeStringRequiredPDF type: <br>- `list`: List<br>- `box`: Box label<br>- `box-qr`: Thermal paper (100x100) (QR code) box label<br>- `carton`: Custom box label
pdf_sizeStringOptionalWhen `pdf_type` equals `list`, optional values:<br> - A4<br> - 216*279<br> - A4-SKU<br><br>When `pdf_type` equals `box`, optional values:<br> - 100*100-WPT (100x100 without product name)<br> - 100*150-WPT (100x150 without product name)<br> - 100*100-PT (100x100 with product name)<br> - 100*150-PT (100x150 with product name)<br> - 100*100-QC (100x100 QR code)<br> - 70*30-B (70x30 with barcode)<br> - 70*30-WB (70x30 without barcode)<br> - A4-SKU (A4 by SKU)<br> - A4-BOX (A4 by box)<br>Only applicable for box labels.<br><br>When `pdf_type` is `box-qr`, this field must contain exactly one box number (e.g., 1). If omitted, box number 1 is used by default.<br><br>When `pdf_type` is `carton` (custom box label), template ID must be provided.
is_eacIntOptionalSet to 1 to display EAC on the box label.<br>Effective only when `pdf_size` is one of:<br>100*100-WPT, 100*150-WPT, 100*100-PT, 100*150-PT<br>EAC is mutually exclusive with SKU barcode, SKU QR code, warehouse code, and custom code.
sku_barcodeIntOptionalSet to 1 to display SKU barcode on the box label.<br>Effective only when `pdf_size` is one of:<br>100*100-WPT, 100*150-WPT, 100*100-PT, 100*150-PT, A4-SKU
goods_barcodeIntOptionalSet to 1 to display warehouse internal code on the box label.<br>Effective only when `pdf_size` is one of:<br>100*100-WPT, 100*150-WPT, 100*100-PT, 100*150-PT
custom_barIntOptionalSet to 1 to display custom code on the box label.<br>Effective only when `pdf_size` is one of:<br>100*100-WPT, 100*150-WPT, 100*100-PT, 100*150-PT
sku_bar_qcIntOptionalSet to 1 to display SKU QR code on the box label.<br>Effective only when `pdf_size` is one of:<br>100*100-WPT, 100*150-WPT, 100*100-PT, 100*150-PT
warehouse_showIntOptionalSet to 1 to display customs declaration type and destination warehouse name on the box label.<br>Effective only when `pdf_size` is one of:<br>100*100-WPT, 100*150-WPT, 100*100-PT, 100*150-PT
content_typeStringOptionalPDF return type, optional values: `url`, `base64`. Default is `base64`.
made_in_chinaIntOptionalWhether to display "Made in China": 0 = Do not display, 1 = Display.<br>Effective only when `pdf_size` is one of:<br>100*100-WPT, 100*150-WPT, 100*100-PT, 100*150-PT, 100*100-QC
temp_idIntOptionalFor `carton` custom box label type, template ID must be provided.<br>Obtain custom box label templates from the basic data interface.
is_ThirdWarehouse_boxIntOptionalWhether to return box label files for third-party warehouses (only valid when `pdf_type=box`).

messageStringRefer to common response parameters

base64StringBase64 encoded PDF content
content_is_urlStringOptional values: `true`, `false`.<br>When `base64` field contains a URL, this is `true`; otherwise, `false`.
ErrorObjectRefer to Error format

forceVerifyintOptionalWhether to force verification (e.g., verify to warehouse system despite arrears or stock shortage): 0 = no, 1 = yes; default is 0. Effective only when verify == 1.

Request
Response
paramsJson Parameters
Parameter NameData TypeRequiredDescription
platformstringRequirePlatform (enum values: yandex, ozon, wildberries)
user_accountstringOptionPlatform store
warehouse_codestringOptionWarehouse code (must be consistent with the audited order). Required for yandex; not required for ozon and wildberries
platform_shipment_nostringRequirePlatform shipment batch number: for yandex, pass Shipmentno from platform store; for wildberries, pass delivery QR code from platform store; for ozon, pass waybill ID
platform_shipment_datestringRequirePlatform shipment batch date (yyyy-mm-dd): for yandex and ozon, pass the platform specified delivery date; not required for wildberries
platform_warehouse_namestringOptionDelivery warehouse name: for yandex and ozon, specify the overseas warehouse for delivery; not required for wildberries
platform_warehouse_addressstringOptionDelivery warehouse address: supported only by Yandex; not required for ozon and wildberries
platform_plan_totalintRequirePlanned shipment quantity: refers to the order quantity in the delivery note for yandex and ozon, and the number of orders in the bag for wildberries
confirmstringRequireWhether to confirm shipment, 1 for yes, 0 for no (confirming shipment requires passing scan_form_file and file_type parameters)
scan_form_filestringRequireMaster document file, base64 encoded
file_typestringRequireFile type, only pdf supported
order_listarrayRequireOrder details

Request - Standard Return

Request - Return by Mail

Response
paramsJson Parameters
Parameter NameData TypeRequiredDescription
dataarrayrequiredBatch data

data Details

Parameter NameData TypeRequiredDescription
data[0]arrayrequiredReturn order data. The first element array contains the parameter headers required for returns; from the second element onward are the corresponding parameter values, similar to rows in an Excel sheet.
data[1]arrayrequiredReturn product data. The first element array contains the parameter headers required for products; from the second element onward are the corresponding parameter values, similar to rows in an Excel sheet.
response Parameters
Parameter NameData TypeDescription
askstringRefer to common response parameters
messagestringRefer to common response parameters
dataObjectData content
data Parameters
Parameter NameData TypeDescription
errorMsgObjectError information
msgstringNumber of successful entries

errorMsg Parameters

Parameter NameData TypeDescription
linestringLine number
msgObjectError message

Edit Last-Mile Delivery Order 编辑落地配订单 Value-Added Services

editPackageFloorOrder

Home > Value-Added Services Module > Edit Package Floor Order

---

Request

---

Response

---

paramsJson Parameters

Parameter NameData TypeRequiredDescription
package_codestringRequiredPackage code
shipping_methodstringRequiredShipping method sm_code
warehouse_codeStringRequiredDestination warehouse CODE
order_codeStringOptionalOrder number. When the configuration `AL_PACKAGE_FLOOR_BY_ORDER` is enabled, the order number is required. It will fill in the order warehouse code and consignee/sender information which cannot be modified. If the configuration is not enabled, the order number information is ignored and consignee/sender information is used instead.
fill_orderintRequiredWhether to fill order information. Default is 0: do not fill; 1: fill. If filled, consignee and sender information cannot be modified.
verifyintRequiredWhether to verify: 0 for create without verification (draft status), 1 for create and verify. Default is 0. Once verified, the order cannot be edited.

---

askstringRefer to common response parameters
messagestringRefer to common response parameters

Response

---

paramsJson Parameters

Parameter NameData TypeRequiredDescription
fba_codeString(32)OptionalFBA order number; update if exists, add if not
reference_numberString(32)OptionalReference number (must be unique)
fba_typeInt(4)RequiredType: 1 - Transit, 2 - Order
fba_idint(11)OptionalFBA warehouse ID (used before version 03, corresponds to the "FBA Address ID" parameter in the Get FBA Warehouse API); send empty if not using FBA warehouse
fba_w_codeString(255)OptionalFBA warehouse code (recommended, corresponds to the "FBA Address CODE" parameter in the Get FBA Warehouse API); send empty if not using FBA warehouse
sm_typeInt(4)Optional(Required for FBA transit) Transit type: 1 - Domestic transit, 2 - Overseas transit, 3 - Overseas relabeling, 4 - Transit stock preparation, 5 - Self-preparation stock
amazon_shipmentstring(64)OptionalAmazon Shipment Id
amazon_referencestring(64)OptionalAmazon Reference Id
to_warehouse_codeString(32)RequiredFor FBA orders: shipping warehouse CODE; for FBA transit: transit warehouse CODE
transit_warehouse_codeString(32)OptionalDelivery warehouse code (required for domestic transit type in FBA transit orders)
stock_typeint(1)RequiredStock type: 0 - Warehouse based, 1 - Standard area, 2 - Transit area, 3 - Return temporary storage area
sm_codestring(64)OptionalDelivery channel (channels blacklisted in WMS cannot be used)
is_insuranceint(1)OptionalInsurance service: 0 - No, 1 - Yes
insurance_valuefloat(10,3)OptionalInsured amount (required if is_insurance is 1)
fba_remarksstring(255)OptionalRemarks
fba_fn_skuObjectOptionalFN SKU details (remove this parameter for standard orders)
boxRowsObjectOptionalBox details (required if fba_type is 1)
productsObjectOptionalProduct details
attachmentsObjectOptionalDocument attachments
is_batch_shipint(1)OptionalWhether to ship in batches: 1 - Yes, 0 - No (default 0)
box_infoObjectOptionalFBA order packing information (required if is_batch_ship is 1)

---

f_askintLabel/attachment upload status; 1 means success (default), 0 means failure; note: empty label/attachment also counts as success
messagestringRefer to common response parameters
dataObjectData content
ErrorObjectRefer to Error format

Message Subscriptions — 数据消息订阅
Message Subscription 消息订阅 Message Subscriptions

Message Subscription

Home > Data Message Subscription > Message Subscription

---

request

Response

---

paramsJson Parameters

Parameter NameData TypeRequiredDescription
subscript_typeStringRequiredSubscription data type, enum values: order - Order, receiving - Receiving order, stock - Stock change, ec_new_fba - New FBA business
callbackStringOptionalCallback URL, optional. After data changes, an HTTP POST request will be sent to notify data retrieval. When enabling subscription, if a callback URL is provided, its validity will be verified. A GET request will be sent to the callback URL with a `random` parameter containing a random number. The callback interface must return this number as-is to confirm connectivity. Example:
[dev@test]#curl 'http://your-erp-domain.com/callback-path?random=1679297714' -H 'Accept: */*' -H 'Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8'
[dev@test]#{"random":"1679297714"}
erp_platformStringRequiredERP platform type, enum values: eccangerp - ECCANG ERP, othererp - Third-party ERP, erp - Self-developed ERP
tenant_idStringOptionalERP tenant ID, required when erp_platform is eccangerp. This will be returned as-is in the callback URL, e.g., `?tenant_id=abc`
expire_dateDateRequiredSubscription expiration date in the format YYYY-MM-DD, e.g., 2023-03-20. Subscription callbacks will only trigger before this date. After expiration, re-subscription is required.

---

Frequently Asked Questions

1. How to fill in the callback URL and what are the requirements?

The callback URL is the key channel for subsequent data change notifications and determines the accuracy of the notifications. Therefore, when setting the callback URL, ensure it is properly accessible.

Requirements:

1. Publicly accessible: The callback URL must be accessible from the public internet without requiring login (security can be ensured via data signature verification).

2. Verification mechanism: The callback URL must be verified. Verification is done by sending an HTTP GET request from outside the network with a random parameter whose value is any random number. If the callback URL returns the same random number, verification passes.

Example:

If the callback URL is set to http://oms-local.com/default/svc-test/msg-subscript-callback, the request would be:

http://oms-local.com/default/svc-test/msg-subscript-callback?random=1679297714

The response should be:

{"random":"1679297714"}

Here, 1679297714 is a user-defined random number that can be set arbitrarily, the key is that it must be returned exactly.

Postman Request Example:

Use Postman to send the request and ensure the correct response is received, as shown in the example image.

You can also test and verify within the OMS system, with the operation shown in the following figure:

---

2. In subscription data types, can I subscribe only to a specific node, for example, subscribing to receiving orders but only want to subscribe to the "receiving order shelving completed" node?

No.

Data subscription callbacks are pushed based on the business document level, and the node structure of each business document may vary. If you only want to subscribe to specific nodes, you can selectively process them based on the node type (type parameter) in the callback notification. For non-target types, you can simply ignore them and respond quickly to achieve this.

---

Request Callback Interface Parameter Example

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<SOAP-ENV:Envelope xmlns:SOAP-ENV="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/" xmlns:ns1="http://www.example.org/Ec/">
	<SOAP-ENV:Body>
		<ns1:callService>
			<paramsJson>
                {
                    "subscript_type" :"receiving",
                    "callback":"http://your-erp-domain.com/callback-path",
                    "erp_platform":"eccangerp",
                    "tenant_id":"ec",
                    "expire_date":"2026-12-31"
                }
            </paramsJson>
			<appToken>xxxxxxxxxxx</appToken>
			<appKey>yyyyyyyyyyyyy</appKey>
			<service>messageSubscript</service>
		</ns1:callService>
	</SOAP-ENV:Body>
</SOAP-ENV:Envelope>

---

Signature Rules

Please refer to the signature rules section for details on how to generate the sign parameter.

---

Common Request Parameters Description

Parameter NameData TypeRequiredDescription
app_keyStringRequiredUser application Key, can be found in OMS Personal Center, same AppKey used for OMS API integration
signStringRequiredSignature string, see signature rules for details
timestampStringRequiredSending time (Linux timestamp)
msg_idStringRequiredMessage ID, unique
subscript_typeStringRequiredSubscription data type, consistent with subscription configuration options. Possible values: `order` (Order), `receiving` (Inbound Order), `stock` (Inventory Change)
bodyObjectRequiredBusiness-level parameters, see the business interface description below

---

Common Response Parameters Description

When the callback request is received, the callback interface must respond with HTTP Status Code 200 to be considered a successful notification.

Parameter NameData TypeRequiredDescription
codeIntRequiredStatus code. 200 - success, others - failure
msgStringRequiredResponse message

---

order (Order Push)

After the callback interface receives the notification, the ERP should call the following APIs for reference:

- getOrderByRefCode (Get single order information by reference number)

- getOrderByCode (Get single order information by order number)

Pass the received order number or reference number as the query condition to fetch the latest data for the single order.

Push Conditions:

a. Push after the shipment tracking number is obtained for the order;

b. Push after the order is checked out and shipped;

c. Push on fee changes or re-billing.

---

Business-level Parameter `body` Description for Order

Parameter NameData TypeRequiredDescription
order_codeStringRequiredOrder number
reference_noStringRequiredCustomer reference number
warehouse_codeStringRequiredWarehouse code
customer_codeStringRequiredCustomer code
order_statusStringRequiredLatest order status at callback time (for reference only, actual status should be based on query results). Enum values:

C: Pending shipment approval

W: Pending shipment

D: Shipped

H: Temporarily saved

N: Exception order

P: Problematic order

X: Discarded |

typeStringRequiredOrder change node, enum:

1: Order information (excluding tracking number, shipment, fee change nodes)

2: Order fee

3: Order tracking number

4: Order shipment

5: Asynchronous order creation |

---

receiving (Inbound Order Push)

After the callback interface receives the notification, the ERP should call the following API:

- getAsnList (Get inbound order list)

Pass the received inbound order number or reference number as the query condition to fetch the latest data for the single inbound order.

Push Conditions:

a. Push after the inbound order is received at the warehouse;

b. Push after the inbound order is shelved at the warehouse;

c. Push after the shelving operation of the inbound order.

---

Business-level Parameter `body` Description for Inbound Order

Parameter NameData TypeRequiredDescription
receiving_codeStringRequiredInbound order number
reference_noStringRequiredCustomer reference number
warehouse_codeStringRequiredWarehouse code
customer_codeStringRequiredCustomer code
receiving_statusStringRequiredLatest inbound order status at callback time (for reference only, actual status should be based on query results). Enum values:

C: Created

W: First leg in transit

P: First leg receiving in progress

T: First leg receiving completed

Z: In transit

G: Destination warehouse receiving in progress

F: Destination warehouse receiving completed

E: Shelving completed

X: Discarded |

typeStringRequiredInbound order change node, enum:

1: Inbound order receiving completed

2: Inbound order shelving completed

3: Inbound order shelving operation |

---

stock (Inventory Change Push)

After the callback interface receives the notification, the ERP should call the following API:

- getProductInventory (Get product inventory)

Pass the received product SKU or reference number along with warehouse code as query conditions to fetch the latest inventory data for the product.

Inventory changes occur on the following events:

a. Warehouse inventory adjustment;

b. Drop-shipping order checkout inventory change;

c. Warehouse stocktaking inventory change;

d. Standard inbound order shelving inventory change;

e. Return shelving inventory change;

f. Problematic item handling inventory change;

g. Destruction order handling inventory change.

---

Business-level Parameter `body` Description for Inventory Change

Parameter NameData TypeRequiredDescription
product_skuStringRequiredProduct SKU
product_barcodeStringRequiredProduct barcode
customer_codeStringRequiredCustomer code
warehouse_codeStringRequiredWarehouse code
reference_noStringRequiredCustomer reference number
business_codeStringRequiredBusiness code of the inventory change document

---

SOAP XML Response Example

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<SOAP-ENV:Envelope xmlns:SOAP-ENV="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/" xmlns:ns1="http://www.example.org/Ec/">
    <SOAP-ENV:Body>
        <ns1:callServiceResponse>
            <response>{"ask":"Success","data":[],"message":"Success"}</response>
        </ns1:callServiceResponse>
    </SOAP-ENV:Body>
</SOAP-ENV:Envelope>

---

Callback Response Example

[dev@test]#curl 'http://your-erp-domain.com/callback-path?random=1679297714' -H 'Accept: */*' -H 'Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8'
[dev@test]#{"random":"1679297714"}

---

This completes the subscription callback interface documentation for ECCANG WMS API.
